module: Cisco-IOS-XE-policy

  augment /ios:native:
    +--rw service-group* [group-id]
       +--rw group-id          uint16
       +--rw description?      string
       +--rw service-policy
          +--rw input?    -> /ios:native/policy/policy-map/name
          +--rw output?   -> /ios:native/policy/policy-map/name
